	focus = {
		id = SOV_Lenin_Cult
		icon = GFX_goal_support_communism
		x = 77
		y = 0
		cost = 10
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}

		allow_branch = {
			date > 1932.12.31
			date < 1949.1.1
		}

		available = {
			RON_can_do_focuses_1936 = yes
			has_government = communism
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_Escalate_the_Purge
				has_completed_focus = SOV_Trotskyite_Coup
			}
		}

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		completion_reward = {

			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = home_of_revolution2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = home_of_revolution2
					add_idea = home_of_revolution
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_idea = home_of_revolution2 } }
				#add_stability = 0.05
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = SOV_infrastructure_effort
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_construct_infrastructure
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_Lenin_Cult }
		x = -4
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = SOV_Lenin_Cult
		cost = 10
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}

		available_if_capitulated = yes

		bypass = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = infrastructure_effort_tt
				all_owned_state = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = infrastructure
						size < 3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = SOV_infrastructure_effort_3Inf }
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}

		completion_reward = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					all_owned_state = {
						NOT = { infrastructure < 5 }
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = infrastructure
							size > 2
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
					set_state_flag = SOV_infrastructure_effort_3Inf
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						free_building_slots = {
							building = infrastructure
							size > 2
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
					set_state_flag = SOV_infrastructure_effort_3Inf
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					infrastructure < 5
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = SOV_infrastructure_effort_3Inf
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					infrastructure < 5
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = SOV_infrastructure_effort_3Inf
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					infrastructure < 5
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = SOV_infrastructure_effort_3Inf
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					infrastructure < 5
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = SOV_infrastructure_effort_3Inf
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = SOV_French_Soviet_Reapproachment
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_military_deal
		prerequisite = { focus = SOV_Escalate_the_Purge }
		x = 28
		y = 1
		cost = 5

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				ai_irrationality > 25
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				ai_irrationality > 35
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				ai_irrationality > 40
			}
		}

		available_if_capitulated = yes
		bypass = {
			OR = {
    				FRA = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
                		NOT = { country_exists = FRA }
                		has_war_with = FRA
            		}
		}
		completion_reward = {

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { has_idea = Anti_Soviet_Interest } }
					FRA = { remove_ideas = Anti_Soviet_Interest }
				}
			}

			USA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = anti_fascist_diplomacy_focus } }
			ENG = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = anti_fascist_diplomacy_focus } }
			FRA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = anti_fascist_diplomacy_focus }
				#Commented Out because France was going communist
				#add_timed_idea = { idea = comintern_influence days = 1095 }
				# It used to add 15%
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = anti_fascist_diplomacy_fascists }
			}
			#add german ai irrationality, minus relations
		}
	}
